md:max-w-[calc(100%_-var(--sidebar-width))]" data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 mb-2"><ol class="flex items-center text-sm"><li><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-started/quickstarts">Home</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-data-in">Ingest data</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><span class="font-semibold">Troubleshooting</span></li></ol></nav></div><div class="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="kafka-connector-troubleshooting-guide" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Kafka connector troubleshooting guide<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-connector-troubleshooting-guide" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>This guide helps you diagnose and resolve common issues with Tinybird&#x27;s Kafka connector. Use the <code>tinybird.kafka_ops_log</code> <a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/service-datasources#tinybird-kafka-ops-log">Service Data Source</a> to monitor errors and warnings in real time.</p><p>For setup instructions and configuration details, see the <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka">Kafka connector documentation</a>.</p><h2 id="quick-error-lookup" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Quick error lookup<a class="headerlink" href="#quick-error-lookup" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Use this table to quickly find errors and their solutions. Errors may appear in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> (Kafka connector operations) or <code>datasources_ops_log</code> (Data Source ingestion operations).</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Error message / symptom</th><th>Category</th><th>Log source</th><th>Solution link</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Connection timeout or broker unreachable</td><td>Connectivity</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-connection-timeout-or-broker-unreachable">Connection timeout</a></td></tr><tr><td>Authentication failed</td><td>Authentication</td><td>kafka_ops_log, datasources_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-authentication-failed">Authentication failed</a></td></tr><tr><td>SSL handshake failed</td><td>SSL/TLS</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-ssltls-certificate-validation-failed">SSL certificate validation</a></td></tr><tr><td>Schema Registry connection failed</td><td>Deserialization</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-schema-registry-connection-failed">Schema Registry</a></td></tr><tr><td>Deserialization failed - Avro</td><td>Deserialization</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-deserialization-failed---avro">Avro deserialization</a></td></tr><tr><td>Deserialization failed - JSON</td><td>Deserialization</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-deserialization-failed---json">JSON deserialization</a></td></tr><tr><td>Offset commit failed</td><td>Consumer group</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-offset-commit-failed-or-consumer-group-conflict">Offset commit</a></td></tr><tr><td>Consumer lag continuously increasing</td><td>Performance</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-consumer-lag-continuously-increasing">Consumer lag</a></td></tr><tr><td>Schema mismatch or type conversion failed</td><td>Schema</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-schema-mismatch-or-type-conversion-failed">Schema mismatch</a></td></tr><tr><td>Materialized View errors</td><td>Schema</td><td>kafka_ops_log, datasources_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-materialized-view-errors">Materialized View errors</a></td></tr><tr><td>Low throughput or processing stall</td><td>Performance</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-low-throughput-or-processing-stall">Low throughput</a></td></tr><tr><td>Uneven partition processing</td><td>Performance</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-uneven-partition-processing">Uneven partitions</a></td></tr><tr><td>Message too large</td><td>Message size</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-message-too-large-or-quarantined-due-to-size">Message size</a></td></tr><tr><td>Compressed message handling</td><td>Message format</td><td>kafka_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-compressed-message-handling">Compression</a></td></tr><tr><td>Unknown topic or partition</td><td>Kafka</td><td>datasources_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-unknown-topic-or-partition">Unknown topic</a></td></tr><tr><td>Group authorization failed</td><td>Authorization</td><td>datasources_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-group-authorization-failed">Group authorization</a></td></tr><tr><td>Topic authorization failed</td><td>Authorization</td><td>datasources_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-topic-authorization-failed">Topic authorization</a></td></tr><tr><td>Unknown partition</td><td>Kafka</td><td>datasources_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-unknown-partition">Unknown partition</a></td></tr><tr><td>Table in readonly mode</td><td>Data Source</td><td>datasources_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-table-in-readonly-mode">Readonly mode</a></td></tr><tr><td>Timeout or memory limit exceeded</td><td>Resource</td><td>datasources_ops_log</td><td><a href="#error-timeout-or-memory-limit-exceeded">Timeout</a></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h2 id="how-to-diagnose-errors" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">How to diagnose errors<a class="headerlink" href="#how-to-diagnose-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Use both <code>kafka_ops_log</code> and <code>datasources_ops_log</code> to diagnose Kafka connector issues:</p><h3 id="check-kafka-connector-operations" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Check Kafka connector operations<a class="headerlink" href="#check-kafka-connector-operations" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query recent errors and warnings from <code>kafka_ops_log</code>:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    partition,
    msg_type,
    msg,
    lag
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
  AND msg_type IN (&#x27;warning&#x27;, &#x27;error&#x27;)
ORDER BY timestamp DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="check-data-source-ingestion-errors" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Check Data Source ingestion errors<a class="headerlink" href="#check-data-source-ingestion-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query errors from <code>datasources_ops_log</code> to see issues during data ingestion:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    event_type,
    result,
    error,
    elapsed_time
FROM tinybird.datasources_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
  AND result = &#x27;error&#x27;
  AND event_type LIKE &#x27;%kafka%&#x27;
ORDER BY timestamp DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This shows errors that occur during the actual data processing phase, even when the Kafka connection itself might be working.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p><strong>Set up automated monitoring</strong>: Connect these diagnostic queries to your monitoring and alerting tools. Query the <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/clickhouse-interface">ClickHouse® HTTP interface</a> directly from tools like Grafana, Datadog, PagerDuty, and Slack. Alternatively, create API endpoints from these queries, or export them in <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/guides/consume-api-endpoints-in-prometheus-format">Prometheus format</a> for Prometheus-compatible tools. Configure your tools to poll these queries periodically and trigger alerts when errors are detected.</p></div></div><p>For detailed monitoring queries, see <a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/kafka-clickhouse-monitoring">Monitor Kafka connectors</a>.</p><h2 id="connectivity-errors" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Connectivity errors<a class="headerlink" href="#connectivity-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="error-connection-timeout-or-broker-unreachable" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Connection timeout or broker unreachable<a class="headerlink" href="#error-connection-timeout-or-broker-unreachable" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>No messages are being processed</li><li>Errors in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> with messages like &quot;Connection timeout&quot; or &quot;Broker unreachable&quot;</li><li>High lag values that continue to increase</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Incorrect <code>KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS</code> configuration</li><li>Network connectivity issues between Tinybird and your Kafka cluster</li><li>Firewall or security group rules blocking access</li><li>Kafka broker is down or unreachable</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Verify bootstrap servers configuration:</strong></p><ul><li>Check that <code>KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS</code> in your <code>.connection</code> file includes the correct host and port</li><li>Ensure you&#x27;re using the advertised listeners address, not the internal broker address</li><li>For multiple brokers, use comma-separated values: <code>broker1:9092,broker2:9092,broker3:9092</code></li><li>For cloud providers, verify you&#x27;re using the public endpoint provided by your Kafka service</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Test connectivity:</strong></p></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb connection data &lt;connection_name&gt;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This command allows you to select a topic and consumer group ID, then returns preview data. This validates that Tinybird can reach your Kafka broker, authenticate, and consume messages.</p><ol start="3"><li><p><strong>Check network configuration:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify firewall rules allow outbound connections from Tinybird to your Kafka cluster</li><li>For AWS MSK, ensure security groups allow inbound traffic on the Kafka port</li><li>For Confluent Cloud, verify network access settings</li><li>For PrivateLink setups (Enterprise), verify the PrivateLink connection is active</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Verify security protocol:</strong></p><ul><li>Ensure <code>KAFKA_SECURITY_PROTOCOL</code> matches your Kafka cluster configuration</li><li>For most cloud providers, use <code>SASL_SSL</code></li><li>For local development, you may use <code>PLAINTEXT</code></li></ul></li></ol><p>For vendor-specific network configuration help, see:</p><ul><li><a href="guides/confluent-cloud-setup">Confluent Cloud setup guide</a></li><li><a href="guides/aws-msk-setup">AWS MSK setup guide</a></li></ul><h3 id="error-authentication-failed" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Authentication failed<a class="headerlink" href="#error-authentication-failed" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Errors in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> with &quot;Authentication failed&quot; or &quot;SASL authentication error&quot;</li><li>Connection check fails with authentication errors</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Incorrect <code>KAFKA_KEY</code> or <code>KAFKA_SECRET</code> credentials</li><li>Wrong <code>KAFKA_SASL_MECHANISM</code> configuration</li><li>Expired credentials or tokens</li><li>For AWS MSK with OAuthBearer, incorrect IAM role configuration</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><strong>Verify credentials:</strong></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb [--cloud] secret get KAFKA_KEY
tb [--cloud] secret get KAFKA_SECRET
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Ensure the secrets match your Kafka cluster credentials.</p><ol start="2"><li><p><strong>Check SASL mechanism:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify <code>KAFKA_SASL_MECHANISM</code> matches your Kafka cluster (PLAIN, SCRAM-SHA-256, SCRAM-SHA-512, or OAUTHBEARER)</li><li>For Confluent Cloud, typically use <code>PLAIN</code></li><li>For AWS MSK with IAM, use <code>OAUTHBEARER</code> with <code>KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_METHOD AWS</code></li><li>For Redpanda, check your cluster&#x27;s configured SASL mechanism</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>For AWS MSK OAuthBearer:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify the IAM role ARN is correct: <code>tb [--cloud] secret get AWS_ROLE_ARN</code></li><li>Check that the IAM role has the correct trust policy allowing Tinybird to assume the role</li><li>Verify the external ID matches between your connection configuration and IAM trust policy</li><li>Ensure the IAM role has the required Kafka cluster permissions (see <a href="index#aws-iam-permissions">AWS IAM permissions</a>)</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Rotate credentials if needed:</strong></p><ul><li>If credentials have expired, update them using <code>tb secret set</code></li><li>Redeploy your connection after updating secrets</li></ul></li></ol><p>For detailed authentication setup, see:</p><ul><li><a href="guides/aws-msk-setup">AWS MSK setup guide</a> for IAM authentication</li><li><a href="guides/confluent-cloud-setup">Confluent Cloud setup guide</a> for API key authentication</li></ul><h3 id="error-ssltls-certificate-validation-failed" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: SSL/TLS certificate validation failed<a class="headerlink" href="#error-ssltls-certificate-validation-failed" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Errors mentioning &quot;SSL handshake failed&quot; or &quot;certificate validation error&quot;</li><li>Connection failures when using <code>SASL_SSL</code> security protocol</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Missing or incorrect CA certificate</li><li>Self-signed certificate not provided</li><li>Certificate expired or invalid</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><strong>Provide CA certificate:</strong></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb [--cloud] secret set --multiline KAFKA_SSL_CA_PEM
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Paste your CA certificate in PEM format.</p><ol start="2"><li><strong>Add certificate to connection file:</strong></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">KAFKA_SSL_CA_PEM &gt;
   {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_SSL_CA_PEM&quot;) }}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Note: This is a <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles#multiple-lines">multiline setting</a>.</p><ol start="3"><li><strong>Verify certificate format:</strong><ul><li>Ensure the certificate is in PEM format (starts with <code>-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----</code>)</li><li>Include the full certificate chain if required</li><li>For Aiven Kafka, download the CA certificate from the Aiven console</li></ul></li></ol><h2 id="deserialization-errors" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Deserialization errors<a class="headerlink" href="#deserialization-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="error-schema-registry-connection-failed" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Schema Registry connection failed<a class="headerlink" href="#error-schema-registry-connection-failed" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Errors in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> mentioning &quot;Schema Registry&quot; or &quot;Failed to fetch schema&quot;</li><li>Messages not being ingested when using Avro or JSON with schema</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Incorrect <code>KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL</code> configuration</li><li>Missing or incorrect Schema Registry credentials</li><li>Schema Registry is unreachable</li><li>Schema not found in Schema Registry</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Verify Schema Registry URL:</strong></p><ul><li>Check that <code>KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL</code> in your <code>.connection</code> file is correct</li><li>For Basic Auth, use format: <code>https://&lt;username&gt;:&lt;password&gt;@&lt;registry_host&gt;</code></li><li>Ensure the URL is accessible from Tinybird&#x27;s network</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Check schema exists:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify the schema exists in your Schema Registry for the topic</li><li>Ensure the schema subject name matches your topic naming convention</li><li>For Confluent Schema Registry, check subject names like <code>{topic-name}-value</code> or <code>{topic-name}-key</code></li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Test Schema Registry access:</strong></p><ul><li>Use curl or similar tool to verify Schema Registry is reachable</li><li>Verify credentials work with Schema Registry API</li></ul></li></ol><p>For more information on schema management, see the <a href="guides/schema-management">schema management guide</a>.</p><h3 id="error-deserialization-failed-avro" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Deserialization failed - Avro<a class="headerlink" href="#error-deserialization-failed-avro" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Warnings in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> with &quot;Deserialization failed&quot; or &quot;Avro parsing error&quot;</li><li>Messages sent to Quarantine Data Source</li><li><code>processed_messages</code> &gt; <code>committed_messages</code> in monitoring queries</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Schema mismatch between message and Schema Registry</li><li>Schema evolution incompatibility</li><li>Incorrect <code>KAFKA_VALUE_FORMAT</code> or <code>KAFKA_KEY_FORMAT</code> configuration</li><li>Corrupted message data</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Verify format configuration:</strong></p><ul><li>Ensure <code>KAFKA_VALUE_FORMAT</code> is set to <code>avro</code> for Avro messages</li><li>Ensure <code>KAFKA_KEY_FORMAT</code> is set to <code>avro</code> if keys are Avro-encoded</li><li>Verify <code>KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL</code> is configured</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Check schema compatibility:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify the message schema matches the schema in Schema Registry</li><li>Check for schema evolution issues (backward/forward compatibility)</li><li>Review Quarantine Data Source to see the actual message that failed</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Inspect quarantined messages:</strong></p></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT *
FROM your_datasource_quarantine
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
ORDER BY timestamp DESC
LIMIT 100
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps you see the actual message content and identify the issue.</p><ol start="4"><li><strong>Schema evolution:</strong><ul><li>Ensure schema changes are backward compatible</li><li>Consider using schema versioning strategies</li><li>Test schema changes in a development environment first</li></ul></li></ol><p>For detailed schema evolution guidance, see the <a href="guides/schema-management">schema management guide</a>.</p><h3 id="error-deserialization-failed-json" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Deserialization failed - JSON<a class="headerlink" href="#error-deserialization-failed-json" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Warnings in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> with &quot;JSON parsing error&quot; or &quot;Invalid JSON&quot;</li><li>Messages in Quarantine Data Source</li><li>Low success rate in throughput monitoring</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Invalid JSON format in message payload</li><li>Schema mismatch with JSONPath expressions</li><li>Missing required fields in JSON</li><li>Incorrect <code>KAFKA_VALUE_FORMAT</code> configuration</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Verify JSON format:</strong></p><ul><li>Check that messages are valid JSON</li><li>Use a JSON validator to test sample messages</li><li>Review Quarantine Data Source for examples of failed messages</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Check JSONPath expressions:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify JSONPath expressions in your Data Source schema match the message structure</li><li>Test JSONPath expressions with sample messages</li><li>Use <code>json:$</code> to store the entire message if you&#x27;re unsure of the structure</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Handle missing fields:</strong></p><ul><li>Use nullable types for optional fields: <code>Nullable(String)</code></li><li>Provide default values in JSONPath: <code>json:$.field DEFAULT &#x27;&#x27;</code></li><li>Consider using a schemaless approach with <code>data String json:$</code> and extract fields later</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Verify format configuration:</strong></p><ul><li>Use <code>json_without_schema</code> for plain JSON messages</li><li>Use <code>json_with_schema</code> only if you&#x27;re using Schema Registry for JSON schemas</li></ul></li></ol><h2 id="offset-and-consumer-group-errors" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Offset and consumer group errors<a class="headerlink" href="#offset-and-consumer-group-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="error-offset-commit-failed-or-consumer-group-conflict" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Offset commit failed or consumer group conflict<a class="headerlink" href="#error-offset-commit-failed-or-consumer-group-conflict" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Data Source only receives messages from the last committed offset</li><li>Multiple Data Sources competing for the same consumer group</li><li>Errors about offset commit failures</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Multiple Data Sources using the same <code>KAFKA_TOPIC</code> and <code>KAFKA_GROUP_ID</code> combination</li><li>Consumer group already in use by another app</li><li>Offset reset behavior not working as expected</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Use unique consumer group IDs:</strong></p><ul><li>Each Data Source must use a unique <code>KAFKA_GROUP_ID</code> for the same topic</li><li>Use environment-specific group IDs: <code>{{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_GROUP_ID&quot;, &quot;prod-group&quot;) }}</code></li><li>For testing, use unique group IDs to avoid conflicts</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Check for duplicate configurations:</strong></p></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
      datasource_id,
      topic,
      count(*) as group_count
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic
HAVING group_count &gt; 1
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps identify if multiple Data Sources are consuming from the same topic.</p><ol start="3"><li><p><strong>Reset offset behavior:</strong></p><ul><li><code>KAFKA_AUTO_OFFSET_RESET=earliest</code> only works for new consumer groups</li><li>If a consumer group already has committed offsets, it resumes from the last committed offset</li><li>To start from the beginning, use a new <code>KAFKA_GROUP_ID</code> or reset offsets in your Kafka cluster</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Best practices:</strong></p><ul><li>Use different <code>KAFKA_GROUP_ID</code> values for development, staging, and production</li><li>Document which consumer groups are in use</li><li>Monitor consumer group activity in your Kafka cluster</li></ul></li></ol><p>For managing consumer groups across environments, see the <a href="guides/cicd-version-control">CI/CD and version control guide</a>.</p><h3 id="error-consumer-lag-continuously-increasing" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Consumer lag continuously increasing<a class="headerlink" href="#error-consumer-lag-continuously-increasing" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Lag values in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> keep growing</li><li>Messages are not being processed fast enough</li><li>Throughput is lower than message production rate</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Message production rate exceeds processing capacity</li><li>Consumer autoscaling not keeping up with load</li><li>Network latency or connectivity issues</li><li>Data Source schema or Materialized View performance issues</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><strong>Monitor lag trends:</strong></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
      datasource_id,
      topic,
      partition,
      max(lag) as current_lag,
      avg(lag) as avg_lag
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
   AND partition &gt;= 0
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic, partition
ORDER BY current_lag DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><ol start="2"><li><p><strong>Verify autoscaling:</strong></p><ul><li>Tinybird&#x27;s serverless Kafka connector automatically scales consumers</li><li>Monitor <code>kafka_ops_log</code> to see partition assignment changes</li><li>If lag continues to increase, there may be a bottleneck in your Data Source or Materialized Views</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Check Data Source performance:</strong></p><ul><li>Review Materialized View queries that trigger on append</li><li>Optimize complex Materialized View queries that may slow down ingestion</li><li>Check for schema issues causing slow parsing</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Analyze throughput:</strong></p></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
      datasource_id,
      topic,
      sum(processed_messages) as processed,
      sum(committed_messages) as committed,
      (sum(committed_messages) * 100.0 / sum(processed_messages)) as success_rate
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Low success rates indicate processing issues.</p><ol start="5"><li><p><strong>Review partitioning strategy:</strong></p><ul><li>Check if partition distribution is even</li><li>Review partition key design if lag is uneven across partitions</li><li>See the <a href="guides/partitioning-strategies">partitioning strategies guide</a> for optimization tips</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Contact support:</strong></p><ul><li>If lag continues to increase despite autoscaling, contact Tinybird support</li><li>Provide <code>kafka_ops_log</code> queries showing the issue</li><li>Include information about message production rates</li></ul></li></ol><p>For performance optimization strategies, see the <a href="guides/performance-optimization">performance optimization guide</a>.</p><h2 id="data-quality-and-schema-errors" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Data quality and schema errors<a class="headerlink" href="#data-quality-and-schema-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="error-schema-mismatch-or-type-conversion-failed" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Schema mismatch or type conversion failed<a class="headerlink" href="#error-schema-mismatch-or-type-conversion-failed" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Warnings in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> about type mismatches</li><li>Messages in Quarantine Data Source</li><li>Low <code>committed_messages</code> compared to <code>processed_messages</code></li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Data type mismatch between message and Data Source schema</li><li>Missing required fields</li><li>Invalid data formats (for example, date strings that can&#x27;t be parsed)</li><li>JSONPath expressions not matching message structure</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Review schema definition:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify column types match the data in messages</li><li>Use appropriate ClickHouse® types (for example, <code>DateTime</code> for timestamps, <code>Int64</code> for large integers)</li><li>Check for nullable vs non-nullable field requirements</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Test with sample messages:</strong></p><ul><li>Use <code>tb sql</code> to test JSONPath expressions with sample data</li><li>Verify date/time formats can be parsed correctly</li><li>Check numeric formats and precision</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Handle data quality issues:</strong></p><ul><li>Use nullable types for fields that may be missing: <code>Nullable(String)</code></li><li>Provide default values: <code>json:$.field DEFAULT 0</code></li><li>Use type conversion functions if needed: <code>toDateTime(JSONExtractString(data, &#x27;timestamp&#x27;))</code></li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Inspect quarantined data:</strong></p><ul><li>Regularly check Quarantine Data Source for patterns</li><li>Identify common data quality issues</li><li>Update schema or data producers to fix root causes</li></ul></li></ol><p>For detailed schema management guidance, see the <a href="guides/schema-management">schema management guide</a>.</p><h3 id="error-materialized-view-errors" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Materialized View errors<a class="headerlink" href="#error-materialized-view-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Warnings in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> mentioning Materialized View errors</li><li>Data ingested but Materialized Views not updating</li><li>Errors in Materialized View queries</li><li>Errors in Materialized View queries affecting ingestion</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Materialized View query errors</li><li>Schema changes breaking Materialized View queries</li><li>Resource constraints (memory, CPU)</li><li>Circular dependencies between Materialized Views</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Check Materialized View queries:</strong></p><ul><li>Review Materialized View pipe definitions</li><li>Test Materialized View queries independently</li><li>Verify queries work with the current Data Source schema</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Monitor Materialized View impact:</strong></p><ul><li>Monitor overall ingestion throughput in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> to see if Materialized Views are slowing down ingestion</li><li>Check for errors in Materialized View queries that may be blocking ingestion</li><li>Review Materialized View query complexity and execution time</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Optimize Materialized View queries:</strong></p><ul><li>Simplify complex aggregations</li><li>Add appropriate filters to reduce data volume</li><li>Consider breaking complex Materialized Views into multiple steps</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Handle schema evolution:</strong></p><ul><li>Update Materialized View queries when Data Source schema changes</li><li>Test Materialized View changes in development first</li><li>Use <code>FORWARD_QUERY</code> to provide default values for new columns</li></ul></li></ol><h2 id="data-source-operation-errors" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Data Source operation errors<a class="headerlink" href="#data-source-operation-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>These errors occur during the data ingestion phase and are logged in <code>datasources_ops_log</code>. They represent problems that happen during actual data processing, even when the Kafka connection itself might be working.</p><h3 id="error-unknown-topic-or-partition" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Unknown topic or partition<a class="headerlink" href="#error-unknown-topic-or-partition" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Error message:</strong></p><ul><li>&quot;KafkaError[UNKNOWN_TOPIC_OR_PART]: Broker: Unknown topic or partition&quot;</li></ul><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Errors in <code>datasources_ops_log</code> with &quot;Unknown topic or partition&quot;</li><li>No messages being ingested</li><li>Topic name errors</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Topic doesn&#x27;t exist in Kafka cluster</li><li>Topic was deleted</li><li>Topic name typo in configuration</li><li>Topic retention policies caused data deletion</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Verify topic exists:</strong></p><ul><li>Check your Kafka cluster to confirm the topic exists</li><li>Use Kafka tools: <code>kafka-topics.sh --list --bootstrap-server &lt;server&gt;</code></li><li>Verify topic name matches exactly (case-sensitive)</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Check topic configuration:</strong></p><ul><li>Ensure topic hasn&#x27;t been deleted</li><li>Verify topic retention policies haven&#x27;t removed all data</li><li>Check if topic was renamed</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Verify Data Source configuration:</strong></p></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">cat &lt;datasource_name.datasource&gt;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Check that <code>KAFKA_TOPIC</code> matches the actual topic name.</p><ol start="4"><li><strong>Create topic if needed:</strong><ul><li>If topic doesn&#x27;t exist, create it in your Kafka cluster</li><li>Ensure proper replication factor and partitions</li><li>Redeploy the Data Source after creating the topic</li></ul></li></ol><p><strong>Note:</strong> If the error specifically mentions a partition (not the topic), see <a href="#error-unknown-partition">Unknown partition</a> in the following section for partition-specific troubleshooting.</p><p><strong>Monitor topic errors:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    error,
    count(*) as error_count
FROM tinybird.datasources_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND result = &#x27;error&#x27;
  AND error LIKE &#x27;%UNKNOWN_TOPIC%&#x27;
GROUP BY timestamp, datasource_id, error
ORDER BY error_count DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="error-authentication-failure-during-ingestion" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Authentication failure (during ingestion)<a class="headerlink" href="#error-authentication-failure-during-ingestion" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Error message:</strong></p><ul><li>&quot;KafkaError[_AUTHENTICATION]: Local: Authentication failure&quot;</li></ul><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Errors in <code>datasources_ops_log</code> with authentication failures</li><li>Connection works initially but fails during ingestion</li><li>Credentials expired or rotated during operation</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>SASL credentials expired or invalid during ingestion</li><li>SSL certificates expired</li><li>Authentication settings changed on Kafka broker</li><li>Credentials rotated but not updated in Tinybird</li><li>Token-based authentication expired mid-operation</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><strong>Verify credentials:</strong></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb [--cloud] secret get KAFKA_KEY
tb [--cloud] secret get KAFKA_SECRET
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Ensure secrets match your Kafka cluster credentials.</p><ol start="2"><li><p><strong>Check for credential expiration:</strong></p><ul><li>Some credentials have expiration dates</li><li>Rotate credentials if they&#x27;ve expired</li><li>Update secrets and redeploy connection</li><li>For token-based auth, ensure tokens are refreshed before expiration</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Verify SSL certificates:</strong></p><ul><li>Check certificate expiration dates</li><li>Update certificates if expired</li><li>Verify certificate format is correct</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Test connection:</strong></p></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb connection data &lt;connection_name&gt;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This validates authentication is working.</p><ol start="5"><li><strong>Check for intermittent auth failures:</strong><ul><li>Monitor <code>datasources_ops_log</code> for authentication error patterns</li><li>If errors occur periodically, credentials may be expiring</li><li>Set up credential rotation before expiration</li></ul></li></ol><p><strong>Note:</strong> This error occurs during data ingestion, not during initial connection. If you see authentication errors during connection setup, see <a href="#error-authentication-failed">Authentication failed</a> in the Connectivity errors section.</p><p><strong>Monitor authentication errors:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    error,
    count(*) as error_count
FROM tinybird.datasources_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND result = &#x27;error&#x27;
  AND error LIKE &#x27;%AUTHENTICATION%&#x27;
GROUP BY timestamp, datasource_id, error
ORDER BY error_count DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="error-group-authorization-failed" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Group authorization failed<a class="headerlink" href="#error-group-authorization-failed" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Error message:</strong></p><ul><li>&quot;KafkaError[GROUP_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED]: Broker: Group authorization failed&quot;</li></ul><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Errors in <code>datasources_ops_log</code> with &quot;Group authorization failed&quot;</li><li>Consumer group lacks permissions</li><li>ACLs not configured correctly</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Consumer group lacks proper authorization</li><li>Kafka ACLs not configured for the consumer group</li><li>Consumer group name doesn&#x27;t match ACL configuration</li><li>Permissions changed on Kafka cluster</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Check Kafka ACLs:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify consumer group has read permissions</li><li>Check ACLs for the specific consumer group ID</li><li>Ensure ACLs allow operations on the topic</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Verify consumer group ID:</strong></p><ul><li>Check the <code>KAFKA_GROUP_ID</code> in your Data Source configuration</li><li>Ensure it matches what&#x27;s configured in Kafka ACLs</li><li>Use consistent naming across environments</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Update ACLs:</strong></p><ul><li>Grant necessary permissions to the consumer group</li><li>Ensure group has access to read from the topic</li><li>Verify group can commit offsets</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Test with different group ID:</strong></p><ul><li>Try a different consumer group ID temporarily</li><li>If it works, the issue is with ACLs for the original group</li><li>Update ACLs for the original group</li></ul></li></ol><p><strong>Monitor authorization errors:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    error,
    count(*) as error_count
FROM tinybird.datasources_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND result = &#x27;error&#x27;
  AND error LIKE &#x27;%GROUP_AUTHORIZATION%&#x27;
GROUP BY timestamp, datasource_id, error
ORDER BY error_count DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="error-topic-authorization-failed" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error: Topic authorization failed<a class="headerlink" href="#error-topic-authorization-failed" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Error message:</strong></p><ul><li>&quot;KafkaError[TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED]: Broker: Topic authorization failed&quot;</li></ul><p><strong>Symptoms:</strong></p><ul><li>Errors in <code>datasources_ops_log</code> with &quot;Topic authorization failed&quot;</li><li>Cannot read from topic</li><li>ACLs not configured for topic access</li></ul><p><strong>Root causes:</strong></p><ol><li>Kafka client lacks permission to read from topic</li><li>Topic ACLs not configured</li><li>Permissions changed on Kafka cluster</li><li>Credentials don&#x27;t have topic access</li></ol><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li><p><strong>Check topic ACLs:</strong></p><ul><li>Verify credentials have read permissions on the topic</li><li>Check ACLs for the specific topic name</li><li>Ensure ACLs allow consumer operations</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Verify credentials:</strong></p><ul><li>Ensure credentials have proper topic access</li><li>Check if topic permissions have changed</li><li>Update credentials if needed</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Update ACLs:</strong></p><ul><li>Grant read permissions to the topic</li><li>Ensure consumer group has topic access</li><li>Verify ACLs are applied correctly</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Test connection:</strong></p></li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb connection data &lt;connection_name&gt;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Select the topic to verify access.</p><p><strong>Monitor topic authorization errors:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    error,
    count(*) as error_count
FROM tinybird.datasources_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND result = &#x27;error&#x27;
  AND error LIKE &#x27;%TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION%&#x27;
